读取叫货目录的数据，进行装箱规则的计算
SELECT pcr.goods_code,pcr.box_gauge,pcr.unit,pcr.template_effective FROM p_call_record pcr
                            WHERE pcr.warehouse_code LIKE '001%' AND pcr.group_name
